help rand
--- help for <strong>rand</strong> ---

 <strong>rand</strong> - Uniformly distributed random numbers
    This MATLAB function returns a random scalar drawn from the uniform
    distribution in the interval (0,1).

    Syntax
      X = <strong>rand</strong>
      X = <strong>rand</strong>(n)
      X = <strong>rand</strong>(sz1,...,szN)
      X = <strong>rand</strong>(sz)

      X = <strong>rand</strong>(___,typename)
      X = <strong>rand</strong>(___,like=p)

      X = <strong>rand</strong>(s,___)

    Input Arguments
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#buiavoq-1-n">n</a> - Size of square matrix
        integer value
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#buiavoq-1-sz1szN">sz1,...,szN</a> - Size of each dimension (as separate arguments)
        integer values
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#buiavoq-1-sz">sz</a> - Size of each dimension (as a row vector)
        integer values
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#buiavoq-1-typename">typename</a> - Data type (class) to create
        "double" (default) | "single"
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#buiavoq-1-p">p</a> - Prototype of array to create
        numeric array
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#mw_7b3a095f-0290-4394-8a40-c09de8009e3e">s</a> - Random number stream
        RandStream object

    Output Arguments
      <a href="matlab:web /Applications/MATLAB_R2025a.app/help/matlab/ref/double.rand.html#mw_db7f9989-8116-4434-bf4c-c5ad2048aef0">X</a> - Output array
        scalar | vector | matrix | multidimensional array

    Examples
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/MatrixofRandomNumbersExample')">Matrix of Random Numbers</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/RandomNumbersWithinSpecifiedIntervalExample')">Random Numbers Within Specified Interval</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/RandomIntegersExample')">Random Integers</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/ResetRandomNumberGeneratorExample')">Reset Random Number Generator</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/ThreeDArrayOfRandomNumbersExample')">3-D Array of Random Numbers</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/SpecifyDataTypeofRandomNumbersExample')">Specify Data Type of Random Numbers</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/CloneSizeFromExistingArrayrandExample')">Size Defined by Existing Array</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/CloneSizeandDataTypefromExistingArrayExample')">Size and Data Type Defined by Existing Array</a>
      <a href="matlab:openExample('matlab/RandomComplexNumbersExample')">Random Complex Numbers</a>

    See also <a href="matlab:help double.randi -displayBanner">randi</a>, <a href="matlab:help double.randn -displayBanner">randn</a>, <a href="matlab:help rng -displayBanner">rng</a>, <a href="matlab:help RandStream -displayBanner">RandStream</a>, <a href="matlab:help sprand -displayBanner">sprand</a>, <a href="matlab:help sprandn -displayBanner">sprandn</a>, <a href="matlab:help randperm -displayBanner">randperm</a>

    Introduced in MATLAB before R2006a
    <a href="matlab:doc rand">Documentation for rand</a>
    <a href="matlab:matlab.lang.internal.introspective.overloads.displayOverloads('rand')">Other uses of rand</a>
